Tikapaṭṭhāna, Part II

[page 069]
                                  69
                           [KUSALATTIKAṂ
                            PAṬICCAVĀRO
                         A. PAṆṆATTIVĀRO.
                  1. Hetupaccayo.  (a) Anulomaṃ.]
     (i) Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjeyya hetupaccayā?
     (ii) Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca akusalo dhammo uppajjeyya hetupaccayā?
     (iii) Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca avyākato dhammo uppajjeyya hetupaccayā?
     Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca
     (iv) . . . kusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?
     (v) . . . akusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?
     (vi) . . . kusalo ca akusalo ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?
     (vii) . . . kusalo ca akusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?
     (viii) Siyā akusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca
          (a) akusalo dhammo, uppajjeyya hetupaccayā?
          (b) kusalo dhammo, uppajjeyya hetupaccayā?
          (c) avyākato dhammo uppajjeyya hetupaccayā?
     Siyā akusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca
          (d) akusalo ca avyākato ca, dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?
          (e) kusalo ca avyākato ca, dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?
          (f) kusalo ca akusalo ca, dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?
          (g) kusalo ca akusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?
     (ix) Siyā avyākataṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca
          (a) avyākato dhammo, uppajjeyya hetupaccayā?
          (b) kusalo dhammo, uppajjeyya hetupaccayā?
          (c) akusalo dhammo, uppajjeyya hetupaccayā?
     Siya avyākataṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca
          (d) kusalo ca avyākato ca, dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?
          (e) akusalo ca avyākato ca, dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?
          (f) kusalo ca akusalo ca, dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?
          (g) kusalo ca akusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?


[page 070]
70                       Kusalattikaṃ
     (x) Siyā kusalañ ca avyākatañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca
          (a) kusalo dhammo, uppajjeyya hetupaccayā?
          (b) akusalo dhammo, uppajjeyya hetupaccayā?
          (c) avyākato dhammo, uppajjeyya hetupaccayā?
          (d) kusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?
          (e) akusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?
          (f) kusalo ca akusalo ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?
          (g) kusalo ca akusalo ca avyākatā ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?
     (xi) Siyā akusalañ ca avyākatañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca
          (a) kusalo dhammo, uppajjeyya hetupaccayā?
          (b) akusalo dhammo, uppajjeyya hetupaccayā?
          (c) avyākato dhammo, uppajjeyya hetupaccayā?
          (d) kusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?
          (e) akusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?
          (f) kusalo ca akusalo ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?
          (g) kusalo ca akusalo ca, avyākato ca dhammā uppajjeyyuṃ hetupaccayā?
     Siyā kusalañ ca akusalañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca
          (a)-(g) as above.
     Siyā kusalañ ca akusalañ ca avyākatañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca
          (a)-(g) as above.
                                2.
     Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjeyya ārammaṇapaccayā? . . .
     Yathā hetupaccayo vitthārito.  Evaṃ ārammaṇapaccayo pi vitthāretabbo vācanā maggena . . . evaṃ adhipatipaccayo . . . avigatapaccayo pi vitthāretabbo vācanā maggena.
                            Ekamūlakaṃ.
     Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjeyya hetupaccayā ārammaṇapaccayā . . . pe . . . hetupaccayā avigatapaccayā ?
                            Dumūlakaṃ.
     Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjeyya hetupaccayā ārammaṇapaccayā adhipatipaccayā . . . pe . . .
hetupaccayā ārammaṇapaccayā avigatapaccayā?
                            Timūlakaṃ.

[page 071]
                            Paṭiccavāro                          71
     Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjeyya hetu-, ārammaṇa-, adhipati-, anantarapaccayā . . .
pe . . . hetu-, ārammaṇa-, adhipati-, avigatapaccayā?
                           Catumūlakaṃ.
     Pañcamūlamūkādikā saṅkhittā.  Ekamūlakaṃ, dumūlakaṃ,
ti-, catu-, pañca-, sabbamūlakaṃ asaṃmuyhantena vitthāretabbaṃ.
                           Hetumūlakaṃ.
                               2-24.
     So for the other paccayas (2-24).
     Ekekassa padassa ekamūlakaṃ, dumūlakaṃ, timūlakaṃ,
catumūlakaṃ, pañcamūlakaṃ, sabbamūlakaṃ asaṃmuyhantena vitthāretabbaṃ.
          Tikañ ca paṭṭhānavaraṃ dukuttamaṃ
          Dukaṃ tikañ ceva tikaṃ dukañ ca
          Tikaṃ tikañ ceva dukaṃ dukañ ca
          Cha anulomamhi nayā sugambhīrā ti.
                         [b. Paccanīyaṃ.]
     Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjeyya na-hetupaccayā? . . . (Yathā anulome hetupaccayo vitthāretabbo, evaṃ paccanīye pi na-hetupaccayo vitthāretabbo).
     Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ . . . na-ārammaṇapaccayā . . .
na adhipatipaccayā . . . pe . . . no-atthipaccayā . . . no-natthipaccayā . . . no-vigatapaccayā . . . no avigatapaccayā? . . .
     Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjeyya na-hetupaccayā na-ārammaṇapaccayā? . . . (Yathā anulome ekekassa padassa ekamūlakaṃ, dumūlakaṃ, timūlakaṃ,
catumūlakaṃ, yāva tevīsatimūlaṃ, evaṃ paccanīye pi vitthāretabbaṃ).
     Tikañ ca . . . (here follows the quatrain as above, substituting cha paccanīyamhi for cha anulomamhi).

[page 072]
72                      Kusalattikaṃ
                      [c. Anulomapaccanīyaṃ.]
     Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjeyya hetupaccayā na-ārammaṇapaccayā . . . akusalo dhammo uppajjeyya. . . .
     (Yathā anulome hetupaccayo vitthārito, evaṃ anulomapaccanīye pi padaṃ vitthāretabbaṃ.)
     Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjeyya hetupaccayā na-adhipatipaccayā? . . . hetupaccayā na-anantarapaccayā? . . . pe . . . hetupaccayā no-avigatapaccayā? . . .
     Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjeyya (a) hetupaccayā ārammaṇapaccayā na-adhipatipaccayā? . . . na-anantarapaccayā ? . . . pe . . . no-avigatapaccayā? . . . (b) hetupaccayā ārammaṇapaccayā adhipatipaccayā na-anantarapaccayā ? . . . hetu-, ārammaṇa-adhipati-paccayā no-avigatapaccayā? . . . pe . . .
     Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjeyya ārammaṇapaccayā . . . avigatapaccayā ? . . . na-hetupaccayā . . . avigatapaccayā ? . . . na-ārammaṇapaccayā . . . avigatapaccayā no-vigatapaccayā . . . avigatapaccayā hetupaccayā na-ārammaṇapaccayā . . . avigatapaccayā?
. . . hetupaccayā no-vigatapaccayā . . . avigatapaccayā ?
. . . hetu-ārammaṇa-paccayā nādhipati-paccayā . . . avigatapaccayā? . . . hetu-ārammaṇa-no-vigata-paccayā . . .
avigatapaccayā ? . . . hetupaccayā ārammaṇapaccayā . . .
pe . . . no-vigatapaccayā? . . .
     Tikañ ca paṭṭhānaṃ . . . pe . . . .
     Cha anuloma-paccanīyamhi nayā sugambhīrā ti.
                        [Paccanīyānulomaṃ.]
     Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjeyya na-hetupaccayā ārammaṇapaccayā ? . . . na-hetupaccayā adhipatipaccayā? . . . pe . . . na-hetupaccayā avigatapaccayā? . . .


[page 073]
                            Paticcavāro                         73
     Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjeyya na-hetupaccayā na-ārammaṇapaccayā adhipatipaccayā . . . pe . . . avigatapaccayā? . . . na-hetupaccayā na-ārammaṇapaccayā na-adhipatipaccayā . . . pe . . . avigatapaccayā? . . . pe . . . no-atthi- . . . no-natthi- . . . novigatapaccayā avigatapaccayā ? . . .
     Siyā kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjeyya nārammaṇapaccayā hetupaccayā ? . . . na-ārammaṇapaccayā adhipatipaccayā? . . . pe . . . na-ārammaṇapaccayā avigatapaccayā? . . . pe . . . no-atthipaccayā hetupaccayā? . . . no-avigatapaccayā ārammaṇapaccayā?
. . . pe . . . no-avigatapaccayā vigatapaccayā? . . . no-avigatapaccayā na-hetupaccayā ārammaṇapaccayā? . . .
no-avigatapaccayā na-hetupaccayā vigatapaccayā? . . .
no-avigatapaccayā na-hetupaccayā na-ārammaṇapaccayā na-adhipatipaccayā?. . . pe . . . no-atthipaccayā no-natthipaccayā vigatapaccayā?
     Tikañ ca paṭṭhānaṃ . . . (the quatrain as above but)
     Cha paccanīyānulomamhi nayā sugambhīrā ti
                      Paṇṇattivāro niṭṭhito.
                         [B. NIDDESAVĀRO.]
                             1 (hetu).
     (i) Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Kusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā,
          tayo khandhe paṭicca eko khandho,
          dve khandhe paṭicca dve khandhā . . .
     (iii) Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca avyākato khandho uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Kusale khandhe paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ . . .


[page 074]
74                          Kusalattikaṃ
     (iv) Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjanti hetupaccayā.
     Kusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ,
          tayo khandhe paṭicca eko khandho citta-, etc.
          dve khandhe paṭicca dve khandhā citta-, etc.
     (viii, a) Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca akusalo dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayo.
     Akusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ . . . (as above).
     (viii, c) Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca avyākato dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Akusale khandhe paṭicca . . . (as above).
     (viii, d) Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca akusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjanti hetupaccayā.
     Akusalaṃ ekaṃ . . . tayo . . . dve . . . (as above).
     (ix, a) Avyākataṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca avyākato dhammo uppajjeyya hetupaccayā.
     Vipākavyākataṃ kiriyāvyākataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ . . . dve khandhe paṭicca dve khandhā citta . . . pe . . .
     Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vipākāvyākataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā kaṭattā ca rūpaṃ . . . tayo khandhe paṭicca eko khandho kaṭattā ca rūpaṃ . . . dve khandhe paṭicca dve khandhā kaṭattā ca rūpaṃ . . . khandhe paṭicca vatthuṃ . . . vatthuṃ paṭicca khandhā . . . ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ paṭicca tayo mahabhūtā . . . tayo mahābhūte paṭicca ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ . . . dve mahābhūte paṭicca dve mahābhūtā . . .
mahābhūte paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ . . . kaṭattārūpaṃ upādā-rūpaṃ . . .
     (x, c) Kusalañ ca avyākatañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca avyākato dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Kusale khandhe ca mahābhūte ca paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ . . .
     (xi, c) Akusalañ ca avyākatañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca avyākato dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Akusale khandhe ca mahābhūte ca paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ . . .

[page 075]
                            Paṭiccavāro                       75
                                2.
     (i) Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjati ārammaṇapaccayā . . . (continue as in 1).
     (viii, a) Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca akusalo dhammo uppajjati ārammaṇapaccayā (continue as under 1, viii, a).
     (ix, a) Avyākataṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca avyākato dhammo uppajjati ārammaṇapaccayā.
     Vipākāvyākataṃ kiriyāvyākataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā . . . tayo khandhe paṭicca eko khandho . . .
dve khandhe paṭicca dve khandhā . . .
     Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vipākāvyākataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā . . . tayo khandhe paṭicca eko khandho . . .
dve khandhe paṭicca dve khandhā . . . vatthuṃ paṭicca khandhā . . .
                                3.
     (i) Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjati adhipatipaccayā . . . (continue as before).
     (iii) Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca avyākato dhammo uppajjati adhipatipaccayā.
     Kusale khandhe paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ . . .
     (iv) Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjanti adhipatipaccayā.
     Kusalaṃ ekaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā cittasamutthānañ ca rūpaṃ . . .
     Kusalaṃ tayo khandhe paṭicca eko khandho cittasamutthānañ ca rūpaṃ . . .
     Kusalaṃ dve khandhe paṭicca dve khandhā cittasamutthānañ ca rūpaṃ . . .
     (viii, a) Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca akusalo dhammo uppajjati adhipatipaccayā.
     . . . ekaṃ . . . tayo . . . tayo . . . ekaṃ . . . dve . . .
dve. . . .
     (viii, c) Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca avyākato dhammo uppajjati adhipatipaccayā.
     Akusale khandhe paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ.
     (viii, d) Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca akusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjanti adhipatipaccayā.


[page 076]
76                       Kusalattikaṃ
     Akusalaṃ ekaṃ . . . (as above 1, c) . . . cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ.
     (ix, a) Avyākataṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca avyākato dhammo uppajjati adhipaṭipaccayā.
     Vipākāvyākataṃ kiriyāvyākataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā.
          tayo khandhe . . . eko . . . samuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ.
          dve khandhe . . . dve . . . samuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ.
     Ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ paṭicca tayo mahābhūtā . . .
          tayo mahābhūte paṭicca ekaṃ mahabhūtaṃ . . .
          dve mahābhūte paṭicca dve mahābhūtā . . .
mahābhūte paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ upādā rūpaṃ.
     (x, c) Kusalañ ca avyākatañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca avyākato dhammo uppajjati adhipatipaccayā.
     Kusale khandhe ca mahābhūte ca paṭicca cittasamutthānaṃ rūpaṃ.
     (xi, c) Akusalañ ca avyākatañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca avyākato dhammo uppajjati adhipatipaccayā.
     Akusale khandhe ca mahābhūte ca paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ . . .
                               4, 5.
     (i) Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca kusalo dhammo uppajjati anantara-paccayā . . . samanantarapaccayā.
     Kusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā . . .
     Anantaraṃ pi samanantaraṃ pi ārammaṇapaccaya-sadisaṃ.
                                6.
     (i) Kusalaṃ . . . kusalo . . . uppajjati sahajātapaccayā.
     Kusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo . . .
          tayo khandhe paṭicca eko  . . .
          dve khandhe paṭicca dve  . . .
     (iii) Kusalaṃ . . . avyākato . . . uppajjati sahajātapaccayā.
     Kusale khandhe paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ.
     (iv) Kusalaṃ . . . kusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjanti sahajātapaccayā.
     Kusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ . . . tayo cittasamuṭṭhanañ ca rūpaṃ.
          tayo  . . . . . . . eko cittasamuṭṭhanañ ca rūpaṃ.
          dve   . . . . . . . dve khandhā cittasamuṭṭhanañ ca rūpaṃ.

[page 077]
                            Paṭiccavāro                         77
     (viii, a) Akusalaṃ . . . akusalo . . . uppajjati sahajātapaccayā.
     (viii, b) Akusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ . . . tayo . . .
                         tayo . . . . . . . . eko . . .
                         dve  . . . . . . . . dve khandhā . . .
     (viii, c) Akusalaṃ . . . avyākato . . . uppajjati sahajātapaccayā.
     Akusale khandhe paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ.
     (viii, d) Akusalaṃ . . . akusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjanti sahajātapaccayā.
     Akusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ . . . tayo . . . cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ.
          tayo  . . . . . . . eko cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ.
          dve   . . . . . . . dve khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ.
     (ix, a) Avyākataṃ . . . avyākato . . . uppajjati sahajātapaccayā.
     Vipākāvyākataṃ kiriyāvyākataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ.
          tayo khandhe . . . eko . . . cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ.
          dve khandhe . . . dve . . . cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ.
     Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vipākāvyākataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā kaṭattā ca rūpaṃ . . .
          . . . tayo khandhā eko . . . kaṭattā ca rūpaṃ.
          . . . dve khandhā dve . . . kaṭattā ca rūpaṃ.
          . . . khandhe paṭicca vatthuṃ . . .
                 vatthuṃ paṭicca khandhā.
     Ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ paṭicca tayo . . .
          tayo . . . . . ekaṃ . . .
          dve  . . . . . dve mahābhūtā . . .
     Mahābhūte paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ kaṭattā rūpaṃ upādā rūpaṃ.
     Bāhiraṃ ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ paṭicca tayo mahābhūtā . . .
          tayo . . . . . . . . .  ekaṃ
          dve . . . . . . . . . . dve
     Mahābhūte paṭicca upādārūpaṃ.

     (iii) Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca avyākato dhammo uppajjati vippayuttapaccayā.

     (c) Khandhe . . . vippayuttapaccayā.

eko . . . kaṭattā ca rūpaṃ . . .; so for dve . . . dve . . .
     Khandhā vatthuṃ, kaṭattā-rūpaṃ khandhe . . . vippayuttapaccayā. Khandhe paṭicca vatthu . . .; vatthuṃ paṭicca khandhā.
     Khandhā vatthuṃ, vatthu khandhe . . . vippayuttapaccayā.

[page 084]
84                       Kusalattikaṃ
                         [Gaṇanā-mūlakā.1]
          Hetuyā nava                   Kamme nava
          Ārammaṇe tīṇi                 Vipāke ekaṃ
          Adhipatiyā nava               Āhāre nava
          Anantare tīṇi                 Indriye nava
          Samanantare tīṇi              Jhāne nava
          Sahajāte nava                 Magge nava
          Aññamaññe tīṇi                Sampayutte tīṇi
          Nissaye nava                  Vippayutte nava
          Upanissaye tīṇi               Atthiyā nava
          Purejāte tīṇi                 Natthiyā tīṇi
          Āsevane tīṇi                  Vigate tīṇi
                                         Avigate nava.
     Hetupaccayā         [Hetumūlakā.]
          ārammaṇe tīṇi            samanantare tīṇi
          adhipatiyā nava          sahajāte nava
          anantare tīṇi            aññamaññe tīṇi . . .
                                    etc., as in list above.
     Hetupaccayā         [Dumūlakaṃ.]
          ārammaṇapaccayā          anantare tīṇi
          adhipatiyā tīṇi          samanantare tīṇi . . .
                   All tīṇi except vipāke ekaṃ.
                           [Timūlakaṃ.]
     Hetupaccayā ārammaṇapaccayā adhipatipaccayā anantara-, samanantara-, sahajāta-, aññamañña-, nissaya-, upanissaya-, purejāta-, āsevana-paccayā kamme tīṇi . . . avigate tīṇi (omitting vipāka-).
                           [Sesamūlakā.]
     Hetupaccayā . . . vigatapaccayā avigatapaccayā tīṇi
     Hetupaccayā . . . pe . . . purejāta-, kamma-, vipāka-,
āhāre ekaṃ . . . avigate ekaṃ.


[page 085]
                            Paṭiccavāro                          85
     Hetupaccayā . . . pe . . . purejātapaccayā kammapaccayā . . . vigatapaccayā avigate ekaṃ.
                    Gaṇanā-hetumūlakā niṭṭhitā.
     Ārammaṇe ṭhitena sabbattha tīṇ' eva pañhā.
     Ārammaṇapaccayā hetuyā tīṇi.
                     adhipatiyā tīṇi . . . pe . . .
                     avigate tīṇi.
     Adhipatipaccayā hetuyā nava
                     ārāmmaṇe tīṇi . . . pe . . .
                     avigate nava.
     Anantarapaccayā hetuyā tīṇi . . . pe . . . avigate tīṇi.
     samanantarapaccayā hetuyā tīṇi . . . pe . . . avigate tīṇi.
     Sahajātapaccayā hetuyā nava . . . pe . . .
     Aññamaññapaccayā hetuyā tīni.
     Nissayapaccayā hetuyā nava,
     Upanissayapaccayā hetuyā tīṇi.
     Purejātapaccayā hetuyā tīṇi,
     Āsevanapaccayā hetuyā tīṇi,
                    ārammaṇe tīṇi . . . pe . . .
                    purejāte tīṇi,
                    kamme tīṇi,
                    āhāre tīṇi . . . pe . . .
                    avigate tīṇi.
          Āsevanamūlake vipākaṃ natthi.
     Kammapaccayā hetuyā nava
     Vipākapaccayā hetuyā ekaṃ,
                   ārammaṇe ekaṃ . . . pe . . .
                   purejāte ekaṃ,
                   kamme ekaṃ
                   āhāre ekaṃ . . . pe . . .
                   avigate ekaṃ.
          Vipākamūlake āsevanaṃ natthi.

[page 086]
86                       Kusalattikaṃ
     Āhārapaccayā hetuyā nava.
     Indiryapaccayā hetuyā nava.
     Jhānapaccayā hetuyā nava.
     Maggapaccayā hetuyā nava.
     Sampayuttapaccayā hetuyā tīṇi,
     Vippayuttapaccayā hetuyā nava,
     Atthipaccayā hetuyā nava,
     Natthipaccayā hetuyā tīṇi
     Vigatapaccayā hetuyā tīṇi
     Avigatapaccayā hetuyā nava,
                    ārammaṇe tīṇi,
                    adhipatiyā nava,
                    natthiyā tīṇi,
                    vigate tīṇi.
     Ekekaṃ paccayaṃ mūlakaṃ kātun asajjhāyantena gaṇetabbā ti.
                             Anulomaṃ.
                           [Paccanīyaṃ.]
                           1 (na-hetu).
     (viii, a) Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca akusalo dhammo uppajjati na-hetupaccayā.

eko . . .; dve . . . dve . . .

                         Paccanīyānulomaṃ.
                       Paṭiccavāro niṭṭhito.
                           [Sahajātavāro
                            Anulomaṃ.]
                                1.
     (i) Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ sahajāto kusalo dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Kusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ sahajātā tayo khandhā; tayo khandhe sahajāto eko khandho; dve khandhe sahajātā dve khandhā.
     (iii) Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ sahajāto avyākato dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Kusale khandhe sahajātaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ.
     (iv) Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ sahajāto kusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjanti hetupaccayā.
     Kusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ.  Sahajātā tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ, tayo khandhe sahajāto eko khandho cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; dve khandhe sahajātā dve khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ.
     (viii, a) Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ sahajāto akusalo dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Akusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ sahajātā tayo khandhā, tayo . . . eko . . .; dve . . . dve khandhā.
     Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ sahajāto avyākato dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Akusale khandhe sahajātaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ.
     (viii, d) Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ sahajāto akusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjanti hetupaccayā.
     Akusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ sahajātā tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; tayo . . . eko . . .; dve . . . dve . . .
     (ix, a) Avyākataṃ dhammaṃ sahajāto avyākato dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.

[page 108]
108                      Kusalattikaṃ
     Vipākāvyākataṃ kiriyāvyākataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ sahajātā tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ tayo . . . eko . . .; dve . . . dve . . .
     Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vipākāvyākataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ sahajātā tayo khandhā kaṭattā ca rūpaṃ; so for tayo . . .
eko . . .; dve . . . dve . . .
     Khandhe sahajātaṃ vatthu; vatthuṃ sahajātā khandhā.
     Ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ sahajātā tayo mahābhūtā; so for tayo . . . ekaṃ . . .; dve . . . dve. . . .  Mahābhūte sahajātaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ kaṭattārūpaṃ upādārūpaṃ.
     (x, c) Kusalañ ca avyākatañ ca dhammaṃ sahajāto avyākato dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Kusale khandhe ca mahābhūte ca sahajātaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ.
     (xi, c) Akusalañ ca avyākatañ ca dhammaṃ sahajāto avyākato dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Akusale khandhe ca mahābhūte ca sahajātaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ.
          Yathā paṭiccavāro evaṃ vitthāretabbaṃ.

110                        Kusalattikaṃ
                          [Paccayavāro.]
                                1.
     (i) Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paccayā kusalo dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Kusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paccayā tayo khandhā tayo khandhe paccayā eko khandho, dve khandhe paccayā dve khandhā.
     (iii) Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paccayā avyākato dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Kusale khandhe paccayā cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ.
     (iv) Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paccayā kusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjanti hetupaccayā.
     Kusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paccayā tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ so for tayo . . .; dve . . . dve . . .
     (viii, a) Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ paccayā akusalo dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Akusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paccayā tayo khandhā; so for tayo . . .; dve . . .
     (viii, c) Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ paccayā avyākato dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Akusale khandhe paccayā cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ.
     (viii, d) Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ paccayā akusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjanti hetupaccayā.
     Akusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paccayā tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ so for tayo . . .; dve . . . dve . . .
     (ix, a) Avyākataṃ dhammaṃ paccayā avyākato dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Vipākāvyākataṃ kiriyāvyākataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paccayā tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; so for tayo . . .;
dve . . .
     Paṭisandhikkhane vipākāvyākataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paccayā tayo khandhā kaṭattā ca rūpaṃ so for tayo . . ., dve . . .
Khandhe paccayā vatthu; vatthuṃ paccayā khandhā.
     Ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ paccayā tayo mahābhūtā; so for tayo . . . dve . . . dve mahābhūtā.  Mahābhūte paccayā cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ kaṭattārūpaṃ upādārūpaṃ.  Vatthuṃ paccayā vipākāvyākatā kiriyāvyākatā khandhā.

     (ix, b) Avyākataṃ dhammaṃ paccayā kusalo dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.

112                         Kusalattikaṃ
     Akusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca vatthuñ ca paccayā tayo khandhā; so for tayo . . .; dve . . . dve . . .
     Akusale khandhe ca mahābhūte ca paccayā cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ.
                                2.
     (i) Kusalaṃ . . . kusalo . . . uppajjati ārammaṇapaccayā.
     Kusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paccayā tayo khandhā; so for tayo . . .; dve . . .
     (viii, a) Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ paccayā akusalo dhammo uppajjati ārammaṇapaccayā.
     Akusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paccayā tayo khandhā; so for tayo . . .; dve . . . paccayā dve khandhā.
     (ix, a) Avyākataṃ dhammaṃ paccayā avyākato dhammo uppajjati ārammaṇapaccayā.
     Vipākāvyākataṃ kiriyāvyākataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paccayā tayo khandhā; so for tayo . . . eko; . . . dve . . . dve . . .
     Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vipākāvyākataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paccayā tayo khandhā; tayo . . . pe . . . dve khandhā.  Vatthuṃ paccayā khandhā.
     Cakkhāyatanaṃ paccayā cakkhuviññāṇaṃ; sotāyatanaṃ paccayā sotaviññāṇaṃ; ghānāyatanaṃ . . . jivhāyatanaṃ . . . kāyāyatanaṃ . . . kāyaviññāṇaṃ.  Vatthuṃ paccayā vipākāvyākatā kiriyāvyākatā khandhā.
     Avyākataṃ dhammaṃ paccayā kusalo dhammo uppajjati ārammaṇapaccayā.
     Vatthuṃ paccayā kusalā khandhā.
     Avyākataṃ . . . akusalo . . . uppajjati ārammaṇapaccayā.
Vatthuṃ paccayā akusalā khandhā.
     (x, a) Kusalañ ca avyākatañ ca dhammaṃ paccayā kusalo dhammo uppajjati ārammaṇapaccayā.
     Kusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca vatthuñ ca paccayā tayo khandhā . . . pe . . . dve khandhā.
     (xi, b) Akusalañ ca avyākatañ ca dhammaṃ paccayā akusalo dhammo uppajjati ārammaṇapaccayā.
     Akusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca vatthuñ ca paccayā tayo khandhā . . . pe . . . dve khandhā.

[page 113]
                           Paccayavāro                          113
                                3.
     Kusalaṃ . . . kusalo . . . uppajjati adhipatipaccayā.
     Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paccayā tīṇi.
     Akusalaṃ . . . akusalo . . . uppajjati adhipatipaccayā.
     Akusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paccayā tīṇi.
     Avyākataṃ . . . avyākato . . . uppajjati adhipatipaccayā.
     Vipākāvyākataṃ kiriyāvyākataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paccayā tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ.
     Ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ paccayā tayo mahābhūtā.  Mahābhūte paccayā cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ upādārūpaṃ.
     Vatthuṃ paccayā vipākāvyākatā kiriyāvyākatā khandhā.

                                     1.
     (viii, a) Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ paccayā akusalo dhammo uppajjati na-hetupaccayā.
     Vicikicchāsahagate uddhaccasahagate khandhe paccayā vicikicchāsahagato uddhaccasahagato moho.
     Avyākataṃ . . . avyākato . . . uppajjati na-hetupaccayā.
     Ahetukaṃ vipākāvyākataṃ kiriyāvyākataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paccayā tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ . . . pe . . . dve khandhe . . . cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ.
     Ahetukapaṭisandhikkhaṇe vipākāvyākataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paccayā tayo khandhā kaṭattā ca rūpaṃ . . . pe . . . dve khandhe paccayā dve khandhā kaṭattā ca rūpaṃ.
     Khandhā paccayā vatthu; vatthuṃ paccayā khandhā.
     Ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ paccayā tayo mahābhūtā . . . pe . . .
mahābhūte paccayā cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ, kaṭattārūpaṃ,
upādārūpaṃ.  Bāhiraṃ; . . . Āhārasamuṭṭhānaṃ . . . Utusamuṭṭhānaṃ . . . Asaññasattānaṃ ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ paccayā tayo mahābhūtā . . . pe . . . Mahābhūte paccayā kaṭattārūpaṃ, upādārūpaṃ.
     Cakkhāyatanaṃ paccayā cakkhuviññāṇaṃ . . . pe . . .
kāyāyatanaṃ paccayā kāyaviññāṇaṃ.  Vatthuṃ paccayā ahetukavipākāvyākatā kiriyāvyākatā khandhā.

[page 123]
                            Paccayavāro                          123
     (ix, c) Avyākataṃ dhammaṃ paccayā akusalo dhammo uppajjati na-hetupaccayā.
     Vatthuṃ paccayā vicikicchāsahagato uddhaccasahagato moho.
     (xi, b) Akusalañ ca avyākatañ ca dhammaṃ paccayā akusalo dhammo uppajjati na-hetupaccayā.
     Vicikicchāsahagate uddhaccasahagate khandhe ca vatthuñ ca paccayā vicikicchāsahagato uddhaccasahagato moho.
                                2.
     Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paccayā avyākato dhammo uppajjati na-ārammaṇapaccayā.
     Kusale khandhe paccayā cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ.
     Yathā paṭiccavāre na-ārammaṇapaccayā evaṃ vitthāretabbaṃ.
                               3.
     (i) Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ paccayā kusalo dhammo uppajjati na-adhipatipaccayā.
     Kusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paccayā . . . (tīṇi).
     (viii) Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ paccayā . . . (tīṇi).
     (ix) Avyākataṃ dhammaṃ paccayā . . .
     Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . . (avyākataṃ paripuṇṇaṃ kātabbaṃ).  Bāhiraṃ . . . Āhārasamuṭṭhānaṃ . . . Utusamuṭṭhānaṃ.  Asaññasattānaṃ ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ paccayā . . .
pe . . .
     Cakkhāyatanaṃ paccayā cakkhuviññāṇaṃ . . . pe . . .
kāyāyatanaṃ paccayā kāyaviññāṇaṃ.  Vatthuṃ paccayā vipākāvyākatā kiriyāvyākatā khandhā.
     (ix, b) Avyākataṃ dhammaṃ paccayā kusalo dhammo uppajjati na-adhipatipaccayā.
     Vatthuṃ paccayā kusalā khandhā . . . pe . . .
          Yathā anulome sahajātapaccayaṃ evaṃ gaṇetabbaṃ.
                          4, 5, 7, 9, 10.
     (iii) Kusalaṃ . . . avyākato dhammo uppajjati na-anantarapaccayā . . . na-samanantarapaccayā, na-aññamaññapaccayā,
na-upanissayapaccayā, na-purejātapaccayā . . . (Yathā paṭiccavāre evaṃ vitthāretabbaṃ).

     Cakkhāyatanaṃ paccayā cakkhuviññāṇaṃ . . . pe . . .

                                13.
     (i) Kusalaṃ . . . kusalo . . . uppajjati na-kammapaccayā.
     Kusale khandhe paccayā kusalā cetanā.
     (viii, a) Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ paccayā akusalo dhammo uppajjati na-kammapaccayā.
     Akusale khandhe paccayā akusalā cetanā.
     (ix, a) Avyākataṃ . . . avyākato . . . dhammo uppajjati na-kammapaccayā.
     Kiriyāvyākate dhamme khandhe paccayā kiriyāvyākatā cetanā.  Bāhiraṃ . . . Āhārasamuṭṭhānaṃ . . . Utusamuṭṭhānaṃ ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ paccayā . . . pe . . . Mahābhūte paccayā upādārūpaṃ.  Vatthuṃ paccayā kiriyāvyākatā cetanā.
     (ix, b) Avyākataṃ dhammaṃ paccayā kusalo dhammo uppajjati na-kammapaccayā.
     Vatthuṃ paccayā kusalā cetanā.
     (ix, c) Avyākataṃ dhammaṃ paccayā akusalo dhammo uppajjati na-kammapaccayā.
     Vatthuṃ paccayā akusalā cetanā.
     (x, a) Kusalañ ca avyākatañ ca dhammaṃ paccayā kusalo dhammo uppajjati na-kammapaccayā.
     Kusale khandhe ca vatthuñ ca paccayā kusalā cetanā.
     (ix, b) Akusalañ ca avyākatañ ca dhammaṃ paccayā akusalo dhammo uppajjati na-kammapaccayā.
     Akusale khandhe ca vatthuñ ca paccayā akusalā cetanā.

                            Paccayavāro                     125
     (ix, a) Avyākataṃ dhammaṃ paccayā avyākato dhammo uppajjati na-vipākapaccayā.
     Kiriyāvyākataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paccayā tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ . . . pe . . . dve khandhe . . .
cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ.
     Ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ paccayā tayo mahābhutā . . . pe . . .
mahābhūte paccayā cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ; upādā rūpaṃ.
Bāhiraṃ . . . Āhārasamuṭṭhānaṃ . . . Utusamuṭṭhānaṃ . . .
Asaññasattānaṃ ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ paccayā tayo mahābhūtā.
. . . Mahābhūte paccayā kaṭattārūpaṃ upādārūpaṃ.  Vatthuṃ paccayā kiriyāvyākatā khandhā.
     (ix, b) Avyākataṃ dhammaṃ paccayā kusalo dhammo uppajjati na-vipākapaccayā.
     Vatthuṃ paccayā kusalā khandhā.
     Vipākaṃ ṭhapetvā sabbattha vitthāretabbaṃ.
                            15-20, 22.
     Avyākataṃ . . . avyākato . . . uppajjati na-āhārapaccayā . . . na-indriyapaccayā, na-jhānapaceayā . . . Cakkhāyatanaṃ paccayā cakkhuviññāṇaṃ . . . pe . . . kāyāyatanaṃ paccayā kāyaviññāṇaṃ . . . Na-jhāne imaṃ nānākaraṇaṃ . . .
na-maggapaccayā:-- Cakkhāyataṇaṃ paccayā cakkhuviññāṇaṃ . . . pe . . . kāyāyatanaṃ paccayā kāyaviññāṇaṃ.
Vatthuṃ paccayā ahetukavipākāvyākatā kiriyāvyākatā khandhā . . . na-magge imaṃ nānākaraṇaṃ; avasesaṃ yathā Paṭiccavāre paccanīyaṃ evaṃ vitthāretabbaṃ . . . na-sampayuttapaccayā . . . na-vippayuttapaccayā . . . no-natthipaccayā . . .

                           Paccayavāro.
                           [NISSAYAVĀRO
                            Anulomaṃ.]
     (i) Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ nissāya kusalo dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Kusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ nissāya tayo khandhā; tayo khandhe nissāya eko khandho; dve khandhe nissāya dve khandhā.
     (iii) Kusalaṃ . . . avyākato . . . uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Kusale khandhe nissāya cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ.
     (iv) Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ nissāya kusalo ca avyākato ca dhamma uppajjanti hetupaccayā.
     Kusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ nissāya tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; tayo . . .; dve . . . cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ.
     (viii, a) Akusalaṃ . . . akusalo . . . uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Akusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ nissāya tayo khandhā . . . pe . . . dve khandhe nissāya dve khandhā.
     (viii, c) Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ nissāya avyākato dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Akusale khandhe nissāya cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ.
     (viii, d) Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ nissāya akusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjanti hetupaccayā.
     Akusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ nissāya tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ . . . pe . . . dve khandhā cittasamutthānañ ca rūpaṃ.
     (ix, a) Avyākataṃ dhammaṃ nissāya avyākato dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Vipākāvyākataṃ kiriyāvyākataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ nissāya tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ . . . pe . . .
dve khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ.
     Paṭisandhikkhane vipākāvyākataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ nissāya tayo khandhā kaṭattā ca rūpaṃ,

138                      Kusalattikaṃ
[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...] tayo . . . dve khandhi kaṭattā ca rūpaṃ.  Khandhe nissāya vatthu; vatthuṃ nissāya khandhā.
     Ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ nissāya tayo mahābhūtā; tayo mahābhūte nissāya ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ; dve . . . dve mahābhūtā.
Mahābhūte nissāya cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ kaṭattā rūpaṃ upādā rūpaṃ.  Vatthuṃ nissāya vipākāvyākatā kiriyāvyākatā khandhā.
     (ix, b) Avyakataṃ . . . kusalo . . . uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Vatthuṃ nissāya kusalā khandhā.
     (ix, c) Avyākataṃ . . . akusalo . . . uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Vatthuṃ nissāya akusalā khandhā.
     (ix, d) Avyākataṃ dhammaṃ nissāya kusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjanti hetupaccayā.
     Vatthuṃ nissāya kusalā khandhā.
     Mahābhūte nissāya cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rupaṃ.
     (ix, e) Avyākataṃ dhammaṃ nissāya akusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjanti hetupaccayā.
     Vatthuṃ nissāya akusalā khandhā.
     Mahābhūte nissāye cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rupaṃ.
     (x, a) Kusalañ ca avyākatañ ca dhammaṃ nissāya kusalo dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Kusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca vatthuñ ca nissāya tayo khandhā . . . pe . . . dve khandhe ca vatthuñ ca nissāya dve khandhā.
     (x, c) Kusalañ ca avyākatañ ca dhammaṃ nissāya avyākato dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Kusale khandhe ca mahābhūte ca nissāya cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ.
     (x, d) Kusalañ ca avyākatañ ca dhammaṃ nissāya kusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā uppajjanti hetupaccayā.
     Kusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca vatthuñ ca nissāya tayo khandhā . . . pe . . . dve khandhe ca vatthuñ ca nissāya dve khandhā.
     Kusale khandhe ca mahābhūte ca nissāya cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ.
     (xi, b) Akusalañ ca avyākatañ ca dhammaṃ nissāya akusalo dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Akusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca vatthuñ ca nissāya tayo khandhā . . . dve khandhā.

     (viii, a) Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ nissāya akusalo dhammo uppajjati na-hetupaccayā.

     Ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ nissāya tayo mahābhūtā, mahābhūte nissāya cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ kaṭattā rūpaṃ, upādā rūpaṃ.

                            Anulomaṃ.]
                                1.
     (i) Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ saṃsaṭṭho kusalo dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Kusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ saṃsaṭṭhā tayo khandhā; tayo khandhe saṃsaṭṭho eko khandho; dve khandhe saṃsaṭṭhā dve khandhā.
     (viii, b) Akusalaṃ dhammaṃ saṃsaṭṭho akusalo dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Akusalaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ saṃsaṭṭhā tayo . . .; dve khandhe . . .
     Avyākataṃ . . . avyākato . . . uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Viriyākāvyākataṃ kiriyāvyākataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ saṃsaṭṭhā tayo khandhā; tayo khandhe . . . dve khandhā.
     Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vipākāvyākataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ saṃsaṭṭhā tayo khandhā, tayo . . . dve khandhā.
                               2, 3.
     Kusalaṃ dhammaṃ saṃsaṭṭho kusalo dhammo uppajjati ārammaṇapaccayā. . . . adhipatipaccayā.
     Paṭisandhikkhaṇe natthi.
     . . . anantarapaccayā,    samanantarapaccayā, sahajātapaccayā, aññamaññapaccayā, nissayapaccayā, upanissayapaccayā: sabbāni padāni hetumūlasadisāni.

dve khandhā.  Vatthuṃ purejātapaccayā.

                          Sampayuttavāro.
     Saṃsaṭṭhattaṃ nāma sampayuttattaṃ; sampayuttattaṃ nāma
                          saṃsaṭṭhattaṃ.
                           [Pañhavāro.]
                                1.
     Kusalo dhammo kusalassa dhammassa hetupaccayena paccayo.
     Kusalo hetu taṃ-sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo.
     Kusalo dhammo avyākatassa dhammassa hetupaccayena paccayo.
     Kusalo hetu cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo.
     Kusalo dhammo kusalassa ca avyākatassa ca dhammassa hetupaccayena paccayo.
     Kusalo hetu-sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo.
     Akusalo dhammo akusalassa dhammassa hetupaccayena paccayo.
     Akusalo hetu taṃ-sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo.


[page 154]
154                      Kusalattikaṃ
     Akusalo dhammo avyākatassa dhammassa hetupaccayena paccayo.
     Akusalo hetu cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo.
     Akusalo dhammo akusalassa ca avyākatassa ca dhammassa hetupaccayena paccayo.
     Akusalo hetu sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo.
     Avyākato dhammo avyākatassa dhammassa hetupaccayena paccayo.
     Vipākāvyākatā kiriyāvyākatā hetū sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo.
     Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vipākāvyākatā hetū sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ kaṭattā ca rūpānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo.
                                2.
     Kusalo . . . kusalassa . . . ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Dānaṃ datvā, sīlaṃ samādiyitvā, uposathakammaṃ katvā,
taṃ paccavekkhati; pubbe suciṇṇāni paccavekkhati; jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā jhānaṃ paccavekkhati; sekhā gotrabhuṃ paccavekkhanti, vodānaṃ paccavekkhanti; sekhā maggā vuṭṭhahitvā maggaṃ paccavekkhanti; sekhā vā puthujjanā vā kusalaṃ aniccato dukkhato anattato vipassanti, cetopariyañāṇena kusalacittasamaṅgissa cittaṃ jānanti.
     Ākāsānañcāyatanakusalaṃ viññaṇañcāyatanakusalassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Ākiñcaññāyatanakusalaṃ nevasaññā-nāsaññāyatanakusalassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Kusalā khandhā iddhividhañāṇassa cetopariyañāṇassa pubbenivāsānussatiñāṇassa yathākammūpagañāṇassa anāgataṃsañāṇassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Kusalo . . . akusalassa . . . ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Dānaṃ datvā, sīlaṃ samādiyitvā, uposathakammaṃ katvā,
taṃ assādeti abhinandati; taṃ ārabbha rāgo uppajjati, diṭṭhi uppajjati, 


[page 155]
                          Pañhavāro                          155
[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...] vicikicchā uppajjati, uddhaccaṃ uppajjati, domanassaṃ uppajjati; pubbe suciṇṇāni assādeti abhinandati;
taṃ ārabbha rāgo uppajjati, diṭṭhi uppajjati, vicikicchā uppajjati, uddhaccaṃ uppajjati, domanassaṃ uppajjati; jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā jhānaṃ assādeti abhinandati; taṃ ārabbha rāgo uppajjati, diṭṭhi uppajjati, vicikicchā uppajjati, uddhaccaṃ uppajjati, jhāne vippaṭisārassa domanassaṃ uppajjati.
     Kusalo . . . avyākatassa . . .ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Arahā maggā vuṭṭhahitvā maggaṃ paccavekkhati, pubbe suciṇṇāni paccavekkhati, kusalaṃ aniccato dukkhato anattato vipassati, cetopariyañāṇena kusalacittasamaṅgissa cittaṃ jhānāti; sekhā vā puthujjanā vā kusalaṃ aniccato dukkhato anattato vipassanti, kusale niruddhe vipāko tad-ārammaṇatā uppajjati; kusalaṃ assādeti abhinandati; taṃ ārabbha rāgo uppajjati, diṭṭhi uppajjati, vicikicchā uppajjati, uddhaccaṃ uppajjati, domanassaṃ uppajjati; akusale niruddhe vipāko tad-ārammaṇatā uppajjati.
     Ākāsānañcāyatanakusalaṃ viññāṇañcāyatanavipākassa ca kiriyassa ca ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.  Ākiñcaññāyatanakusalaṃ nevasaññā-nāsaññāyatanavipākassa ca kiriyassa ca ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Kusalā khandhā cetopariyañāṇassa pubbenivāsānussatiñāṇassa yathākammūpagañāṇassa anāgataṃsañāṇassa āvajjanāya ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Akusalo . . . akusalassa . . . ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Rāgaṃ assādeti abhinandati; taṃ ārabbha rāgo uppajjati,
diṭṭhi . . . vicikicchā . . . uddhaccaṃ . . . domanassaṃ uppajjati; diṭṭhiṃ assādeti abhinandati; taṃ ārabbha rāgo uppajjati . . . pe . . . vicikicchaṃ ārabbha vicikicchā uppajjati, diṭṭhi . . . uddhaccaṃ . . . diṭṭhi . . . domanassaṃ uppajjati; uddhaccaṃ ārabbha uddhaccaṃ uppajjati, vicikicchā . . . domanassaṃ ārabbha domanassaṃ uppajjati, vicikicchā uppajjati, uddhaccaṃ uppajjati.
     Akusalo . . . kusalassa . . . ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Sekhā pahīnakilese paccavekkhanti, vikkhambhitakilese paccavekkhanti, pubbe samudāciṇṇe kilese jānanti.  Sekhā vā puthujjanā vā akusalaṃ aniccato dukkhato anattato vipassanti, cetopariyañāṇena akusalacittasamaṅgissa cittaṃ jānanti.

[page 156]
156                      Kusalattikaṃ
     Akusalā khandhā cetopariyañāṇassa pubbenivāsānussatiñaṇassa yathākammūpagañāṇassa anāgataṃsañāṇassa āvajjanāya ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Akusalo . . . avyākatassa . . . ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Arahā pahīnakilese paccavekkhati, pubbe samudāciṇṇe kilese jānāti, akusalaṃ aniccato dukkhato anattato vipassati, cetopariyañāṇena akusalacittasamaṅgissa cittaṃ jānāti.
Sekhā vā puthujjanā vā akusalaṃ aniccato dukkhato anattato vipassanti.
     Akusale niruddhe vipāko tad-ārammaṇatā uppajjati.  Akusalaṃ assādeti abhinandati; taṃ ārabbha rāgo uppajjati, diṭṭhi . . . vicikicchā . . . uddhaccaṃ . . . domanassaṃ uppajjati.
Akusale niruddhe vipāko tad-ārammaṇatā uppajjati.  Akusalā khandhā cetopariyañāṇassa pubbenivāsānussatiñāṇassa yathākammūpagañāṇassa anāgataṃsañāṇassa āvajjanāya ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Avyākato . . . avyākatassa . . . ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Arahā phalaṃ paccavekkhati, nibbānaṃ paccavekkhati.
Nibbānaṃ phalassa āvajjanāya ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
Arahā cakkhuṃ aniccato dukkhato anattato vipassati, sotaṃ,
ghānaṃ, jivhaṃ, kāyaṃ, rūpe, sadde, gandhe, rase, phoṭṭhabbe,
vatthuṃ . . .
     Vipākāvyākate kiriyāvyākate khandhe aniccato dukkhato anattato vipassati, dibbena cakkhunā rūpaṃ passati, dibbāya sotadhātuyā saddaṃ suṇāti, cetopariyañāṇena vipākāvyākatakiriyāvyākatacittasamaṅgissa cittaṃ jānāti.
     Ākāsānañcāyatanakiriyaṃ viññāṇañcāyatanakiriyassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo. Ākiñcaññāyatanakiriyaṃ nevasaññā-nāsaññāyatanakiriyassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Rūpāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.  Saddāyatanaṃ cetoviññāṇassa, gandhāyatanaṃ ghānaviññāṇassa; rasāyatanaṃ jivhāviññāṇassa, phoṭṭhabbāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Avyākatā khandhā iddhividhañāṇassa cetopariyañāṇassa pubbenivāsānussatiñāṇassa anāgataṃsañāṇassa āvajjanāya ārammaṇapacceyan paccayo.
     Avyākato . . . kusalassa . . . ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.

[page 157]
                             Pañhavāro                             157
     Sekhā phalaṃ paccavekkhanti nibbānaṃ paccavekkhanti.
Nibbānaṃ gotrabhussa vodānassa dhammassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Sekhā vā puthujjanā vā cakkhuṃ aniccato dukkhato anattato vipassanti, sotaṃ ghānaṃ . . . rūpe . . . sadde . . .
vatthuṃ . . . vipākāvyākate kiriyāvyākate khandhe aniccato dukkhato anattato vipassanti; dibbena cakkhunā rūpaṃ passanti, dibbāya sotadhātuyā saddaṃ suṇanti, cetopariyañāṇana vipākāvyākata-kiriyāvyākata-cittasamaṅgissa cittaṃ jānanti.
     Avyākatā khandhā iddhividhañāṇassa cetopariyañāṇassa pubbenivāsānussatiñāṇassa anāgataṃsañāṇassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Ayvākato . . . akusalassa . . . ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo
     Cakkhuṃ assādeti abhinandati; taṃ ārabbha rāgo uppajjati, diṭṭhi . . . vicikicchā . . . uddhaccaṃ . . . domanassaṃ uppajjati.  Sotaṃ . . . ghānaṃ . . . rūpe . . . phoṭṭhabbe vatthuṃ . . .
     Vipākāvyākate kiriyāvyākate khandhe assādeti abhinandati, taṃ ārabbha rāgo uppajjati, diṭṭhi . . . vicikicchā . . .
uddhaccaṃ . . . domanassaṃ uppajjati.
                                3.
     Kusalo dhammo kusalassa . . . adhipati p. paccayo.
     (a) Ārammaṇādhipati, (b) Sahajātādhipati.
     (a) Ārammaṇādhipati:-- dānaṃ datvā, sīlaṃ samādiyitvā uposathakammaṃ katvā taṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhati,
pubbe suciṇṇāni garuṃ katvā paccavekkhati, jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā jhānaṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhati; sekhā gotrabhuṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhanti, vodānaṃ paccavekkhanti;
sekhā maggā vuṭṭhahitvā maggaṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhanti.
     (b) Sahajātādhipati :-- kusalādhipati sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     Kusalo dhammo akusalassa . . . adhipatip. paccayo.
     (a) Dānaṃ datvā, sīlaṃ samādiyitvā, uposathakammaṃ katvā, 


[page 158]
158                           Kusalattikaṃ
[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...] taṃ garuṃ katvā assādeti abhinandati; taṃ garuṃ katvā rāgo uppajjati, diṭṭhi uppajjati.  Pubbe suciṇṇāni garuṃ katvā assādeti abhinandati; taṃ garuṃ katvā rāgo uppajjati, diṭṭhi uppajjati.  Jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā jhānaṃ garuṃ katvā assādeti abhinandati; taṃ garuṃ katvā rāgo . . . diṭṭhi uppajjati.
     Kusalo dhammo avyākatassa . . . adhipatip. paccayo.
     (a, b):-- (a) Arahā maggā vuṭṭhahitvā maggaṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhati.  (b) Kusalādhipati cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     Kusalo dhammo kusalassa ca avyākatassa ca dhammassa adhipatip. paccayo.
     (b) Kusalādhipati sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     Akusalo dhammo akusalassa . . . adhipatip. paccayo.
     (a, b):-- (a) Rāgaṃ garuṃ katvā assādeti abhinandati; taṃ garuṃ katvā rāgo uppajjati diṭṭhi uppajjati; diṭṭhiṃ garuṃ katvā . . . (as above) . . . (b) Akusalādhipati sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     Akusalo dhammo avyākatassa adhipatip. paccayo.
     (b) Akusalādhipati cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     Akusalo dhammo akusalassa ca avyākatassa ca dhammassa adhipatip. paccayo.
     (b) Akusalādhipati sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     Avyākato dhammo avyākatassa . . . adhipatip. paccayo.
     . . . (a, b):-- (a) Arahā phalaṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhati,
nibbānaṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhati.  Nibbānaṃ phalassa adhipatipaccayena paccayo.  (b) Vipākāvyākatā kiriyāvyākatā adhipati sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     Avyākato dhammo kusalassa adhipatip. paccayo.
     (a) Sekhā phalaṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhanti, nibbānaṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhanti.  Nibbānaṃ gotrabhussa vodānassa maggassa adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     Avyākato dhammo akusalassa . . . adhipatip. paccayo.
     (a) Cakkhuṃ garuṃ katvā assādeti abhinandati; taṃ garuṃ katvā rāgo uppajjati, 

[page 159]
                             Pañhavāro                        159
[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...] diṭṭhi uppajjati.  Sotaṃ . . . rūpe . . .
sadde . . . vatthuṃ . . . vipākāvyākate kiriyāvyākate khandhe garuṃ katvā assādeti abhinandati; taṃ garuṃ katvā rāgo uppajjati.
                                4.
     Kusalo dhammo kusalassa anantarap. paccayo.
     Purimā purimā kusalā khandhā pacchimānaṃ pacchimānaṃ kusalānaṃ khandhānaṃ anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     Anulomaṃ gotrabhussa, anulomaṃ vodānassa, gotrabhu maggassa, vodānaṃ maggassa anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     Kusalo dhammo avyākatassa . . . anantarap. paccayo.
     Kusalaṃ vuṭṭhānassa, maggo phalassa, sekhānaṃ anulomaṃ phalasamāpattiyā, nirodhā vuṭṭhahantassa nevasaññā-nāsaññāyatanakusalaṃ phalasamāpattiyā anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     Akusalo dhammo akusalassa anantarap. paccayo.
     Purimā purimā akusalā khandhā pacchimānaṃ pacchimānaṃ akusalānaṃ khandhānaṃ anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     Akusalo dhammo avyākatassa anantarap. paccayo.
     Akusalaṃ vuṭṭhānassa anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     Avyākato dhammo avyākatassa . . . anantarap. paccayo.
     Purimā purimā vipākāvyākatā kiriyāvyākatā khandhā pacchimānaṃ pacchimānaṃ vipākāvyākatānaṃ kiriyāvyākatānaṃ khandhānaṃ anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     Bhavaṅgaṃ āvajjanāya, kiriyaṃ vuṭṭhānassa, arahato anulomaṃ phalasamāpattiyā, nirodhā vuṭṭhahantassa nevasaññā-nāsaññāyatanakiriyaṃ phalasamāpattiyā anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     Avyākato dhammo kusalassa anantarap. paccayo.
     Āvajjanā kusalānaṃ khandhānaṃ anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     Avyākato dhammo kusalassa anantarap. paccayo.
     Āvajjanā akusalānaṃ khandhānaṃ anantarapaccayena paccayo.

160                      Kusalattikaṃ

     Purimā purimā kusalā khandhā pacchimānaṃ pacchimānaṃ kusalānaṃ khandhānaṃ samanantarapaccayena paccayo.
     Anulomaṃ gotrabhussa, anulomaṃ vodānassa, gotrabhu maggassa, vodānaṃ maggassa samanantarapaccayena paccayo.
     Kusalo dhammo avyākatassa . . . samanantarap. paccayo.
     Kusalaṃ vuṭṭhānassa, maggo phalassa, sekhānaṃ anulomaṃ phalasamāpattiyā, nirodhā vuṭṭhahantassa nevasaññā-nāsaññāyatanakusalaṃ phalasamāpattiyā samanantarapaccayena paccayo.
     Akusalo dhammo akusalassa . . . samanantarap. paccayo.
     Purimā purimā akusalā khandhā pacchimānaṃ pacchimānaṃ akusalānaṃ khandhānaṃ samanantarapaccayena paccayo.
     Akusalo dhammo avyākatassa . . . samanantarap. paccayo.
     Akusalaṃ vuṭṭhānassa samanantarapaccayena paccayo.
     Avyākato dhammo avyākatassa . . . samanantarap. paccayo.
     Purimā purimā vipākāvyākatā kiriyāvyākatā khandhā pacchimānaṃ pacchimānaṃ vipākāvyākatānaṃ kiriyāvyākatānaṃ khandhānaṃ samanantarapaccayena paccayo.
     Bhavaṅgaṃ āvajjanāya, kiriyaṃ vuṭṭhānassa, arahato anulomaṃ phalasamāpattiyā, nirodhā vuṭṭhahantassa nevasaññā-nāsaññāyatanakiriyaṃ phalasamāpattiyā samanantarapaccayena paccayo.
     Avyākato dhammo kusalassa . . . samanantarap. paccayo.
     Āvajjanā kusalānaṃ khandhānaṃ samanantarapaccayena paccayo.
     Avyākato dhammo akusalassa samanantarap. paccayo.
     Āvajjanā akusalānaṃ khandhānaṃ samanantarapaccayena paccayo.

                                9.
     Kusalo dhammo kusalassa dhammassa upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     (a) Ārammaṇūpanissayo, (b) anantarūpanissayo, (c) pakatūpanissayo.
     (a) Dānaṃ datvā, sīlaṃ samādiyitvā, uposathakammaṃ katvā, taṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhati; pubbe suciññāni garuṃ katvā paccavekkhati; jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā, jhānaṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhati; sekhā gotrabhuṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhanti; vodānaṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhanti; sekhā maggā vuṭṭhahitvā, maggaṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhanti.
     (b) Purimā purimā kusalā khandhā pacchimānaṃ pacchimānaṃ kusalānaṃ khandhānaṃ upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
Anulomaṃ gotrabhussa, anulomaṃ vodānassa, gotrabhu maggassa, vodānaṃ maggassa upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     (c) Saddhaṃ upanissāya, dānaṃ deti, sīlaṃ samādiyati, uposathakammaṃ karoti: jhānaṃ uppādeti, vipassanaṃ . . .
maggaṃ . . . abhiññaṃ . . . samāpattiṃ uppādeti.
     Sīlaṃ, sutaṃ, cāgaṃ, paññaṃ upanissāya dānaṃ deti, sīlaṃ samādiyati . . . (as above).  Saddhā, sīlaṃ, sutaṃ, cāgo,
paññā saddhāya, sīlassa, sutassa, cāgassa, paññāya upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     Paṭhamassa jhānassa parikammaṃ paṭhamassa jhānassa upanissayapaccayena paccayo; dutiyassa jhānassa parikammaṃ dutiyassa jhānassa upanissayapaccayena paccayo; . . .
(so for tatiyaṃ and catutthaṃ jhānaṃ).
     Ākāsānañcāyatanassa parikammaṃ ākāsānañcāyatanassa upanissap. paccayo; . . . (so for viññāṇañcāyatanaṃ, ākiñcaññāyatanaṃ, nevasaññānāsaññāyatanaṃ).
     Paṭhamaṃ jhānaṃ dutiyassa jhānassa . . . catutthassa jhānassa upanissayap. paccayo.  Catutthaṃ jhānaṃ ākāsānañcāyatanassa, ākāsānañcāyatanaṃ . . . pe . . . nevasaññānāsaññāyatanassa upanissap. paccayo.
     Dibbassa cakkhussa parikammaṃ dibbassa cakkhussa.
Upanissayapaccayena paccayo.  Dibbāya sotadhātuyā parikammaṃ dibbāya sotadhātuyā, iddhividhañāṇassa parikammaṃ iddhividhañāṇassa, 


[page 166]
166                      Kusalattikaṃ
[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...] cetopariyañāṇassa parikammaṃ cetopariyañāṇassa, pubbenivāsānussatiñāṇassa parikammaṃ pubbenivāsānussatiñāṇassa, yathākammupagañāṇassa parikammaṃ yathākammūpagañāṇassa, anāgataṃsañāṇassa parikammaṃ anāgataṃsañāṇassa upanissayapaccayena paccayo
     Dibbaṃ cakkhuṃ dibbāya sotadhātuyā, dibbā sotadhātu iddhividhañāṇassa, iddhividhañāṇaṃ cetopariyañāṇassa,
cetopariyañāṇaṃ pubbenivāsānussatiñāṇassa, pubbenivāsānussatiñāṇaṃ yathākammūpagañāṇassa yathākammūpagañāṇaṃ anāgataṃsañāṇassa upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     Paṭhamassa maggassa parikammaṃ paṭhamassa maggassa upanissayapaccayena paccayo . . . (so for the 2nd to 4th Paths.).
     Paṭhamo maggo dutiyassa maggassa upanissayapaccayena paccayo.  Dutiyo maggo tatiyassa, tatiyo maggo catutthassa maggassa upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     Sekhā maggaṃ upanissāya anuppannaṃ samāpattiṃ uppādenti uppannaṃ samāpajjanti saṅkhāre aniccato dukkhato anattato vipassanti.  Maggo sekhānaṃ atthapaṭisambhidāya dhammapaṭisambhidāya niruttipaṭisambhidāya paṭibhāṇapaṭisambhidāya ṭhānāṭhānakosallassa upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     Kusalo dhammo akusalassa . . . upanissayap. paccayo.
     (a) Ārammaṇūpanissayo, (c) pakatūpanissayo.
     (a) Dānaṃ datvā, sīlaṃ samādiyitvā, uposathakammaṃ datvā, taṃ garuṃ katvā assādeti abhinandati; taṃ garuṃ katvā rāgo uppajjati, diṭṭhi uppajjati.  Pubbe suciṇṇāni taṃ garuṃ katvā assādeti abhinandati, taṃ garuṃ katvā rāgo uppajjati,
diṭṭhi uppajjati; jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā jhānaṃ garuṃ katvā assādeti abhinandati, taṃ garuṃ katvā rāgo . . . diṭṭhi uppajjati.
     (c) Saddhaṃ upanissāya mānaṃ jappeti; diṭṭhiṃ gaṇhāti.
Sīlaṃ, sutaṃ, cāgaṃ, paññaṃ upanissāya mānaṃ jappeti, diṭṭhiṃ gaṇhāti.  Saddhā, sīlaṃ, sutaṃ, cāgo, paññā rāgassa, dosassa,
mohassa, mānassa, diṭṭhiyā, patthanāya upanissayapaccayena paccayo.


[page 167]
                             Pañhavāro                              167
     Kusalo dhammo avyākatassa . . . upanissayap. paccayo.
     (a) Ārammaṇūpanissayo, (b) anantarūpanissayo, (c) pakatūpanissayo.  (a) Arahā maggā vuṭṭhahitvā maggaṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhati.  (b) Kusalaṃ vuṭṭhānassa, maggo phalassa, sekhānaṃ anulomaṃ phalasamāpattiyā, nirodhā vuṭṭhāhantassa nevasaññā -nāsaññāyatanakusalaṃ phalasamāpattiyā upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     (c) Saddhaṃ upanissāya attānaṃ ātāpeti paritāpeti, pariyiṭṭhimūlakaṃ dukkhaṃ paccanubhoti.  Sīlaṃ, sutaṃ, cāgaṃ, paññaṃ upanissāya attānaṃ . . . pe . . . Saddhā, sīlaṃ, sutaṃ, cāgo,
paññā, kāyikassa sukhassa kāyikassa dukkhassa phalasamāpattiyā upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     Kusalaṃ kammaṃ vipākassa upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     Arahā maggaṃ upanissāya anuppannaṃ kiriyasamāpattiṃ uppādeti, uppannaṃ samāpajjati, saṅkhāre aniccato dukkhato anattato vipassati.  Maggo arahato atthapaṭisambhidāya dhammapaṭisambhidāya niruttipaṭisambhidāya paṭibhāṇapaṭisambhidāya ṭhānāṭhānakosallassa . . . Maggo phalasamāpattiyā upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     Akusalo dhammo akusalassa upanissayap. paccayo.
     (a) Ārammanūpanissayo, (b) anantarūpanissayo, (c) pakatūpanissayo:-- (a) Rāgaṃ garuṃ katvā assādeti abhinandati taṃ garuṃ katvā rāgo . . . diṭṭhi uppajjati.  Diṭṭhiṃ garuṃ katvā . . . rāgo uppajjati.
     (b) Purimā purimā akusalā khandhā pacchimānaṃ pacchimānaṃ akusalānaṃ khandhanaṃ upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     (c) Rāgaṃ upanissāya pāṇaṃ hanati, adinnaṃ ādiyati, musā bhaṇati, pisuṇaṃ bhaṇati, pharusaṃ bhaṇati, samphaṃ palapati, sandhiṃ chindati, nillopaṃ harati, ekāgārikaṃ karoti paripanthe tiṭṭhati, paradāraṃ gacchati, gāmaghātaṃ karoti,
nigamaghātaṃ karoti, mātaraṃ jīvitā voropeti, pitaraṃ jīvitā voropeti, arahantaṃ jīvitā voropeti, duṭṭhena cittena tathāgatassa lohitaṃ uppādeti, saṅghaṃ bhindati.  Dosaṃ upanissāya . . . mohaṃ, mānaṃ, diṭṭhiṃ, patthanaṃ upanissāya pāṇaṃ hanati . . . pe . . . saṅghaṃ bhindati.  Rāgo, doso,

moho, māno, diṭṭhi, patthanā rāgassa dosassa mohassa mānassa diṭṭhiyā patthanāya upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     Pāṇātipāto pāṇātipātassa upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
Pāṇātipāto adinnādānassa, kāmesu micchācārassa, musāvādassa, pisuṇāvācāya, pharusāvācāya, samphappalāpassa,
abhijjhāya vyāpādassa, micchādiṭṭhiyā upanissayapaccayena paccayo.  Adinnādānaṃ adinnādānassa, kāmesu micchācārassa musāvādassa . . . saṅkhittaṃ . . . micchādiṭṭhi pāṇātipātassa upanissayapaccayena paccayo . . . cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ.
     Kāmesu micchācāro, musāvādo, pisuṇavācā, pharusavācā,
samphappalāpo, abhijjhā, vyāpādo, micchādiṭṭhi micchādiṭṭhiyā upanissayapaccayena paccayo, micchādiṭṭhi pāṇātipātassa adinnādānassa . . . vyāpādassa upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     Mātughātakammaṃ mātughātakammassa upanissayapaccayena paccayo.  Matūghātakammaṃ pitughātakammassa arahantaghātakammassa ruhiruppādakammassa saṅghabhedakammassa niyatamicchādiṭṭhiyā upanissayapaccayena paccayo. Pitughātakammaṃ pitughātakammassa . . . pe . . . arahantaghātakammassa ruhiruppādakammassa saṅghabhedakammassa niyatamicchādiṭṭhiyā mātughātakammassa upanissayapaccayena paccayo.  Arahantaghātakammaṃ . . .
ruhiruppādakammaṃ . . . saṅghabhedakammaṃ . . . niyatamicchādiṭṭhi niyatamicchādiṭṭhiyā upanissayapaccayena paccayo.  Niyatamicchādiṭṭhi mātughātakammassa . . . arahantaghātakammassa ruhiruppādakammassa saṅghabhedakammassa upanissayapaccayena paccayo . . . (cakkaṃ kātabbaṃ).
     Akusalo dhammo kusalassa . . . upanissayap. paccayo.
     (c) Pakatūpanissayo:-- rāgaṃ upanissāya dānaṃ deti, sīlaṃ samādiyati, uposathakammaṃ karoti; jhānaṃ uppādeti,
vipassanaṃ uppādeti, maggaṃ . . . abhiññaṃ . . . samāpattiṃ uppādeti.  So for dosaṃ, mohaṃ, mānaṃ, diṭṭhiṃ, patthanaṃ.

sutassa, cāgassa, paññāya upanissayapaccayena paccayo.

     Avyākato dhammo avyākatassa purejātap. paccayo.
     (a) Ārammaṇapurejātaṃ, (b) vatthupurejātaṃ.
     (a) Arahā cakkhuṃ aniccato dukkhato anattato vipassati.
Sotaṃ . . . rūpe . . . vatthuṃ aniccato dukkhato anattato vipassati, dibbena cakkhunā rūpaṃ passati, dibbāya sotadhātuyā saddaṃ suṇāti.  Rūpāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa purejātapaccayena paccayo.  Saddāyatanaṃ sotaviññāṇassa . . . phoṭṭhabbāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa purejātapaccayena paccayo.
     (b) Cakkhāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa . . . sotāyatanaṃ sotaviññāṇassa . . . kāyāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa purejātapaccayena paccayo.  Vatthu vipakāvyākatānaṃ kiriyāvyākatānaṃ khandhānaṃ purejātapaccayena paccayo.
     Avyākato dhammo kusalassa . . . purejātap. paccayo.
     (a) Ārammaṇapurejātaṃ, (b) vatthupurejātaṃ.
     (a) Sekhā vā puthujjanā vā cakkhuṃ aniccato dukkhato anattato vipassanti.  Sotaṃ . . . rūpe . . . vatthu aniccato dukkhato anattato vipassanti, dibbena cakkhunā rūpaṃ passanti, dibbāya sotadhātuyā saddaṃ suṇanti.
     (b) Vatthu kusalānaṃ khandhānaṃ purejātapaccayena paccayo.
     Avyākato dhammo akusalassa . . . purejātap. paccayo.
     (a, b):-- (a) Cakkhuṃ assādeti abhinandati; taṃ ārabbha rāgo, diṭṭhi, vicikicchā, uddhaccaṃ, domanassaṃ uppajjati.
Sotaṃ . . . rūpe . . . vatthuṃ assādeti abhinandati; taṃ ārabbha rāgo . . . domanassaṃ uppajjati.
     (b) Vatthu akusalānaṃ khandhānaṃ purejātapaccayena paccayo.

     Vipākāvyākatā kiriyāvyākatā indriyā sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ indriya . . .
Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vipākāvyākatā indriyā sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ kaṭattā ca rūpānaṃ indriya . . . Cakkhundriyaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa indriyapaccayena paccayo.  Sotindriyaṃ sotaviññāṇassa . . . kāyindriyaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa indriyapaccayena paccayo.  Rūpajīvitindriyaṃ kaṭattā-rūpānaṃ indriyapaccayena paccayo.
                                17.
     Kusalo dhammo kusalassa . . . jhānap. paccayo.
     Kusalāni jhānangāni sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ jhānapaccayena paccayo.
     Kusalo dhammo avyākatassa . . . jhānap. paccayo.
     Kusalāni jhānangāni cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ jhānapaccayena paccayo.
     Kusalo dhammo kusalassa ca avyākatassa ca dhammassa jhānap. paccayo.
     Kusalāni jhānangāni sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ jhānap.
     Akusalo dhammo akusalassa . . . jhānap. paccayo.
     Akusalāni jhānangāni sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ jhānapaccayena paccayo.
     Akusalo dhammo avyākatassa . . . jhānap. paccayo.
     Akusalāni jhānangāni cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ jhānapaccayena paccayo.
     Akusalo dhammo akusalassa ca avyākatassa ca dhammassa jhānap. paccayo.
     Akusalāni jhānangāni sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ jhānapaccayena paccayo.
     Avyākato dhammo avyākatassa . . . jhānap. paccayo.
     Vipākāvyākatāni kiriyāvyākatāṇi jhānangāni sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ jhānapaccayena paccayo.  Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vipākāvyākatāni jhānangāni sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ kaṭattā ca rūpānaṃ jhānapaccayena paccayo.

[page 176]
176                      Kusalattikaṃ
                                18.
     Kusalo dhammo kusalassa . . . maggap. paccayo.
     Kusalāni maggangāni sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ maggapaccayena paccayo. . . .   (Each sentence similar to those for Jhānapaccaya.)
                                19.
     Kusalo dhammo kusalassa . . . sampayuttap. paccayo.
     Kusalo eko khandho tiṇṇaṃ khandhānaṃ sampayuttapaccayena paccayo; tayo khandhā ekassa . . . dve khandhā dvinnaṃ khandhānaṃ sampayuttapaccayena paccayo.
     Akusalo dhammo akusalassa . . . sampayuttap. paccayo.
     Akusalo eko khandho . . . (as above).
     Avyākato dhammo avyākatassa . . . sampayuttap. paccayo.
     Vipākāvyākato kiriyāvyākato eko khandho . . . (as above).
                                20.
     Kusalo dhammo avyākatassa . . . vippayuttap. paccayo.
     (a) Sahajātaṃ, (b) pacchājātaṃ.
     (a) Sahajātā kusalā khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.
     (b) Pacchājātā kusalā khandhā purejātassa imassa kāyassa vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.
     Akusalo dhammo avyākatassa . . . vippayuttap. paccayo.
     (a, b):-- (a) Sahajātā akusalā khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.
     (b) Pacchājātā akusalā khandhā purejātassa imassa kāyassa vippayuttap. paccayo.
     Avyākato dhammo avyākatassa . . . vippayuttap. paccayo.
     (a) Sahajātaṃ, (b) purejātaṃ, (c) pacchājātaṃ.
     (a) Vipākāvyākatā kiriyāvyākatā khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.  Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vipākāvyākatā khandhā kaṭattārūpānaṃ vippayutta. . . .  Khandhā vatthussa . . . vatthu khandhānaṃ vippayutta . . .
     (b) Cakkhāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa vippayutta . . .
sotāyatanaṃ sotaviññāṇassa . . . kāyāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa vippayutta . 

[page 177]
                             Pañhavāro                       177
[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...] . . vatthu vipākāvyākatānaṃ kiriyāvyākatānaṃ khandhānaṃ vippayutta . . .
     (c) Vipākāvyākatā kiriyāvyākatā khandhā purejātassa imassa kāyassa vippayuttap. paccayo.
     Avyākato dhammo kusalassa . . . vippayuttap. paccayo.
     (b) Vatthu kusalānaṃ khandhānaṃ vippayutta . . .
     Avyākato dhammo akusalassa . . . vippayuttap. paccayo.
     (b) Vatthu akusalānaṃ khandhānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.
                                21.
     Kusalo dhammo kusalassa . . . atthipaccayena paccayo.
     Kusalo eko khandho tiṇṇaṃ khandhānaṃ, tayo khandhā ekassa khandhassa, dve khandhā dvinnaṃ khandhānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.
     Kusalo dhammo avyākatassa . . . atthip. paccayo.
     (a) Sahajātaṃ, (b) pacchājātaṃ.
     (a) Kusalā khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.
     (b) Kusalā khandhā purejātassa imassa kāyassa atthipaccayena paccayo.
     Kusalo dhammo kusalassa ca avyākatassa ca dhammassa atthipaccayena paccayo.
     Kusalo eko khandho tiṇṇaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ, tayo khandhā ekassa . . . dve khandhā dvinnaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ atthip. . . .
     Akusalo dhammo akusalassa . . . atthip. paccayo.
     Akusalo eko khandho tiṇṇaṃ, dve dvinnaṃ khandhānaṃ atthip. paccayo.
     Akusalo dhammo avyākatassa . . . atthip. paccayo.
     (a, b):-- (a) Akusalā khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ atthi . . .
     (b) Akusalā khandhā purejātassa imassa kāyassa atthipaccayena paccayo.
     Akusalo dhammo akusalassa ca avyākatassa ca dhammassa atthip. paccayo.
     Akusalo eko khandho tiṇṇaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ . 

[page 178]
178                      Kusalattikaṃ
[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...] . . dve . . . dvinnaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ atthi . . .
     Avyākato dhammo avyākatassa . . . atthip. paccayo.
     (a) Sahajātaṃ, (b) purejātaṃ, (c) pacchājātaṃ (1) āhāraṃ,
(2) indriyaṃ.
     (a) Sahajāto vipākāvyākato kiriyāvyākato eko khandho tiṇṇaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ . . .
dve . . . dvinnaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ atthi . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vipākāvyākato eko khandho tiṇṇaṃ khandhānaṃ kaṭattā ca rūpānaṃ . . . dve . . . dvinnaṃ khandhānaṃ kaṭattā ca rūpānaṃ atthi. . . .  Khandhā vatthussa, vatthu khandhānaṃ atthi.  Ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ tiṇṇaṃ mahabhūtānaṃ . . . dve . . . dvinnaṃ mahābhūtānaṃ atthi. . . .  Mahābhūtā cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ kaṭattā ca rūpānaṃ upādārūpānañ ca atthipaccayena paccayo.  Bāhiraṃ . . . Āhārasamuṭṭhānaṃ . . . Utusamuṭṭhānaṃ . . . Asaññasattānaṃ ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ tiṇṇaṃ mahābhūtānaṃ atthi. . . .  Mahābhūtā [cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ] kaṭattā ca rūpānaṃ upādārūpānañ ca atthipaccayena paccayo.
     (b) Arahā cakkhuṃ aniccato dukkhato anattato vipassati;
sotaṃ . . . rūpe . . . vatthuṃ aniccato dukkhato anattato vipassati; dibbena cakkhunā rūpaṃ passati, dibbāya sotadhātuyā saddaṃ suṇāti.
     Rūpāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa atthipaccayena paccayo.
Saddāyatanaṃ . . . pe . . . phoṭṭhabbāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa atthi. . . . Cakkhāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa atthi. . . .  Sotāyatanaṃ sotaviññāṇassa. . . .  Kāyāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa atthi. . . .  Vatthu vipākāvyākatānaṃ kiriyāvyākatānaṃ khandhānaṃ atthi. . . .
     (c) Pacchājātā vipākāvyākatā kiriyavyākatā khandhā purejātassa imassa kāyassa atthi. . . .  Kabaḷiṅkāro āhāro imassa kāyassa atthi. . . .  Rūpajīvitindriyaṃ kaṭattā-rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.
     Avyākato dhammo kusalassa . . . atthip. paccayo.
     (b) Sekhā vā puthujjanā va cakkhuṃ aniccato dukkhato anattato vipassanti;

                             Pañhavāro                          179
[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...] sotaṃ . . . rūpe . . . vatthuṃ aniccato dukkhato anattato vipassanti; dibbena cakkhunā rūpaṃ passanti; dibbāya sotadhātuyā saddaṃ suṇanti. Vatthuṃ kusalānaṃ khandhānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.
     Avyākato dhammo akusalassa . . . atthip. paccayo.
     (b) Purejātaṃ cakkhuṃ assādeti abhinandati; taṃ ārabbha rāgo, diṭṭhi, vicikicchā, uddhaccaṃ, domanassaṃ uppajjati;
sotaṃ . . . pe . . . ghānaṃ . . . rūpe . . . vatthuṃ assādeti abhinandati; taṃ ārabbha rāgo uppajjati . . . pe . . . domanassaṃ uppajjati.  Vatthuṃ akusalānaṃ khandhānaṃ atthi. . . .
     Kusalo ca avvyākato ca dhammā kusalassa dhammassa atthip. paccayo.
     (a) Sahajāto kusalo eko khandho ca vatthuñ ca tiṇṇaṃ khandhānaṃ atthi . . . pe . . . dve khandhā ca vatthuñ ca dvinnaṃ khandhānaṃ atthi. . . .
     Kusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā avyākatassa dhammassa atthip. paccayo.
     (a) Sahajātaṃ, (b) pacchājātaṃ, (c) āhāraṃ, (d) indriyaṃ.
     (a) Kusalā khandhā ca mahābhūtā ca cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ atthi. . . .
     (b, c) Kusalā khandhā ca kabaliṅkāro āhāro ca imassa kāyassa atthi. . . .
     (b, d) Kusalā khandhā ca rūpajīvitindriyañ ca kaṭattārūpānaṃ atthi . . .
     Akusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā akusalassa dhammassa atthip. paccayo.
     Sahajāto akusalo eko khandho ca vatthuñ ca tiṇṇaṃ khandhānaṃ . . . tayo khandhā ca vatthuñ ca ekassa khandhassa . . . dve khandhā ca vatthuñ ca dvinnaṃ khandhānaṃ atthi. . . .
     Akusalo ca avyākato ca dhammā avyākatassa dhammassa atthip. paccayo.
     (a, b, c, d):-- (a) Akusalā khandhā ca mahābhūtā ca cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ atthi. . . .
     (b, c) Akusalā khandhā ca kabaḷiṅkāro āhāro ca imassa kāyassa atthi. . . .
     (b, d) Akusalā khandhā ca rūpajīvitindriyañ ca kaṭattā-rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.
